  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d0ad9eef-b213-400c-876e-3cefca79175b'
      });

  <span id="freeText7068037383606137869" style="display:none">**Recommended for ages 17+ due to sexual content and language, mature subject matter**<br /><br />New Adult Contemporary<br /><br />Lost. That one single word best describes my life at this very moment. I lost the last games of the season and both my team and my coach blame me. I lost the last two months because I drowned in my own despair like a complete loser. And I lost the only girl who ever mattered because I was afraid being with me would destroy her.<br /><br />But now I realize how truly lost I am without her. She has become my story…and even though she acts like she’s moved on, I know she still thinks about me just as much as I think about her. She’s beautiful, sweet—and so damn vulnerable, all I want to do is help her. Be there for her.<br /><br />Love her…<br /><br />If only I could convince Fable to give me a second chance. Then I wouldn’t feel so lost anymore, and neither would she. We could be found together.<br /><br />Forever.</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">He was under the age of consent, so that makes it molestation. Molestation is fondling, which we can safely assume she did, and Stagitory Rape is when<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">He was under the age of consent, so that makes it molestation. Molestation is fondling, which we can safely assume she did, and Stagitory Rape is when th act of sex occurs between the minor and the adult.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13251268046390236151">Um, I'm not trying to be an ego maniac by giving my own book 5 stars but I just wanted to let everyone know a few things about SECOND CHANCE BOYFRIEND...<br/><br/>-- There will be no cliffhanger. This book wraps up Drew + Fable's story.<br/><br/>-- It will be LONGER. Much longer.<br/><br/>-- It will be SEXIER. Much sexier. I've come to realize that Drew + Fable can't keep their hands off each other.<br/><br/>-- Release date is scheduled for **EDITED TO ADD** April 9th (SORRY EVERYONE ONLY ONE MORE WEEK TO WAIT!).<br/><br/>-- Just because this i</span>
  <span id="freeText13251268046390236151" style="display:none">Um, I'm not trying to be an ego maniac by giving my own book 5 stars but I just wanted to let everyone know a few things about SECOND CHANCE BOYFRIEND...<br /><br />-- There will be no cliffhanger. This book wraps up Drew + Fable's story.<br /><br />-- It will be LONGER. Much longer.<br /><br />-- It will be SEXIER. Much sexier. I've come to realize that Drew + Fable can't keep their hands off each other.<br /><br />-- Release date is scheduled for **EDITED TO ADD** April 9th (SORRY EVERYONE ONLY ONE MORE WEEK TO WAIT!).<br /><br />-- Just because this is the sequel doesn't mean I won't continue in this world. There's a character who's in this book and I love him. He needs his own book. So he shall be getting one.<br /><br />-- Am I the only one who thinks eventually Owen deserves his own book too? I hope not. *winks*</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525722231?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525722231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4402436362517620479">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>4.5 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: New Adult Romance<br/><b>Full review posted on 4/7/13</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408036i/797782.jpg' alt=' photo 8a921644-6c32-47cd-9c0a-cacc59de49f6_zpsb02bc685.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>'Drew Callahan is my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can’t get enough of. He’s my addiction and if I’m being honest with myself, I’m not looking to kick that particular habit anytime soon.'</b> ~Fable<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408036ra/797783.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mh1cxkFS2h1s3mhmuo1_500_zpse49ff3a9.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>This book was just shy of the 5 STAR mark for me. <br/>Did I love it? <u>HELL YES!</u><br/>Do I think other readers will love it? <u>HELL YES!</u><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408036i/797784._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 071bc0ecd74bacc04a0c29c970a4b47c_zps1771b803.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i>“My mom was pretty dead on when she named me F</i></span>
  <span id="freeText4402436362517620479" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4.5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><b>Full review posted on 4/7/13</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408036i/797782.jpg" alt=" photo 8a921644-6c32-47cd-9c0a-cacc59de49f6_zpsb02bc685.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>'Drew Callahan is my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can’t get enough of. He’s my addiction and if I’m being honest with myself, I’m not looking to kick that particular habit anytime soon.'</b> ~Fable<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408036ra/797783.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mh1cxkFS2h1s3mhmuo1_500_zpse49ff3a9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>This book was just shy of the 5 STAR mark for me. <br>Did I love it? <u>HELL YES!</u><br>Do I think other readers will love it? <u>HELL YES!</u><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408036i/797784._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 071bc0ecd74bacc04a0c29c970a4b47c_zps1771b803.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>“My mom was pretty dead on when she named me Fable, wasn’t she? I don’t feel real to anyone.”</i><br> <i>“You’re real to me,” </i>I whisper. So damn real, it hurts not to touch her.<br><br>When this book starts two months have past since Fable has seen Drew. And once they finally lay eyes on each other again he knows he cannot continue his path of loneliness. It’s time for him to admit what he did was wrong. It’s time to get his girl back.<br><br><b>Marshmallow</b><br><br> A boys night out causes Drew to call on Fable when he finds himself to drunk to drive. She picks him up and takes him home and then stays the night. Drew apologizes for his actions after their one week together. They talk and follow it up with earth shattering sex. <br><br><i>‘She holds my heart in her hands. <br>And for the first time in my life, <br>I give it over to her completely. <br>Freely.<br>Fable Maguire owns me. And I know I own her.’</i> ~Drew<br><br>These two sizzle on the pages, I wish we could have gotten a little more of them as a couple, doing couple things such as dating. Life seems to just get in the way, everything for these two as a couple moves forward. Unfortunately their personal lives outside of being a couple has them both in emotional turmoil. <br>Things go from really bad to extremely horrible for Fable and Owen on the home front. Having to keep Owen on the straight and narrow plus deal with their BITCH of a mother is <b>NOT</b> easy. She clings to Drew in her time of need yet still remains her independent self by not relying on a man to get things done. <br>Drew battles with his secrets as his father reaches out to him as a confidant. Drew's fear of no longer having his father in his life if those secrets come to life cause him to be constantly on edge. Meanwhile Fable is a steady guide and strong life line in his time of need.<br><br><b>The truth is rarely pure and never simple. – Oscar Wilde</b><br><br>As you read on you start to get that “uh oh” feeling, like you know shit is about to hit the fan. And then it does. And it happens in a way I was not expecting.<u> AT</u><u> ALL.</u><br><br><b>Highlights</b><br><br>-A punch to the jaw<br>-Game of True Confessions<br>-Sex against the wall<br>-A surprise POV switch<br><br><b>In my humble opinion -One of the best lines written in 2013</b><br><br><i>‘Now, we own the happily ever after and we refuse to let that bitch go.’</i> ~Fable<br><br>Love this chick!<br><br><br><b>My Casting:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408036i/797785.jpg" alt=" photo b5291d77-77bc-4ce6-a372-dff9e29ffc24_zps4a524e83.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408036i/797786.jpg" alt=" photo 6258adab-4b4f-42dd-bbfc-3176419ba186_zps64bea7ad.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My Thoughts<br>I <b>love love love</b> these characters. I love how Murphy kept Fable’s independent spirit in tact even when she hit the bottom of her sanity. I love how Drew was respectful of her spirit; how he was gentle with her needs and tender in the way he cared for her and she with him. I loved Drew’s vulnerability, how he had it all but didn’t at the same time… Because he allowed his past to haunt his thoughts and fill him with guilt.<br><br>I stopped myself from giving this book five stars because a story line that has been burnt in to my brain was not resolved. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Was Drew the father of Adele's daughter???? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I’m curious to see the reactions of readers to Adele and her part in this book…<br><br>I highly doubt this is the end of Drew and Fable. Meaning we will most likely see them featured in another book as supporting cast mates to a new couple…<br><b> Not my idea of an HEA,</b> but it does have a happy ending. Ok, so my idea of an HEA is a nice flash in to the future. You get marriage, a house, maybe 2.5 kids.. You get my drift right?! This story gives a flash forward in to their near future and just ends on a happy note. Also as I previously stated, I do foresee more books in the near future. We meet two new characters(Colin and Jen) that will grab your attention strictly based on the dynamics of their relationship...or lack there of. PLUS, I would love to get a book for Owen. You'll understand why once you read it.<br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Loved most hated others<br>Writing Style- Savory <br>Plot/Storyline- Emotionally charged with good sexy moments<br>Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br>Overall- I loved it!! READ IT!!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><br>*Copy kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review*</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8211592653242473379"><b>5 Stars</b><br/><br/>LOVED IT! <br/>Now here is my Drew...<br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/SecondChanceboyfriend-Drewshirtlessredone_zpsd75f7b96.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>It’s been a few months since Drew left Fable in her apartment... they haven’t communicated or seen one another since. But that doesn’t mean they have forgotten one another and the time they spent together. Drew is <br/><blockquote>
<b>Lost. That one single word describes my life at this very moment.</b> </blockquote><br/>and spending his time in class writing poems about Fable. <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/SecondChanceBoyfriend-Marshamallowredone_zpseb61b16f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408077i/797959.jpg' alt=' photo SecondChanceBoyfriend-Marshamallowredone_zpseb61b16f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>He is talking to a therapist, trying to get himself together. He misses Fable like crazy. She was the one real thi</span>
  <span id="freeText8211592653242473379" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars</b><br><br>LOVED IT! <br>Now here is my Drew...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/SecondChanceboyfriend-Drewshirtlessredone_zpsd75f7b96.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408077i/797958.jpg" alt=" photo SecondChanceboyfriend-Drewshirtlessredone_zpsd75f7b96.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s been a few months since Drew left Fable in her apartment... they haven’t communicated or seen one another since. But that doesn’t mean they have forgotten one another and the time they spent together. Drew is <br><blockquote>
<b>Lost. That one single word describes my life at this very moment.</b> </blockquote><br>and spending his time in class writing poems about Fable. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/SecondChanceBoyfriend-Marshamallowredone_zpseb61b16f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408077i/797959.jpg" alt=" photo SecondChanceBoyfriend-Marshamallowredone_zpseb61b16f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>He is talking to a therapist, trying to get himself together. He misses Fable like crazy. She was the one real thing in his life. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“My mom was pretty dead on when she named me Fable, wasn’t she? I don’t feel real to anyone.” “You’re real to me.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/SecondChanceboyfriend-Fableredone_zpsc6982285.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408077i/797960.jpg" alt=" photo SecondChanceboyfriend-Fableredone_zpsc6982285.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Fable is heartbroken, but she has to move on, has to survive, even if she is dying inside. Fable has a little brother who counts on her, so she continues to work hard. She even gets a new job at an upscale restaurant making much better tips than before. One night while working, he comes in...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/SecondChanceBoyfriend-Drew1redone_zpsda6253c1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408077i/797961.jpg" alt=" photo SecondChanceBoyfriend-Drew1redone_zpsda6253c1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><blockquote>
  <b>Drew Callahan in my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can’t get enough of. He’s my addiction. </b>
</blockquote><br>That night, they throw everything out there. They talk. They get back together. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/SecondChanceBoyfriend-kissredone_zpsd7463ef9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408077i/797962.jpg" alt=" photo SecondChanceBoyfriend-kissredone_zpsd7463ef9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was <u>so happy</u> we didn’t have to wait and wait for Drew and Fable to be together. They are much stronger now then they were in the first book. Although they have just as many (if not more) obstacles than before. Not only is the crazy bitch back- and CRAZIER than ever, they have to deal with Fable’s mom, and her little brother. Plus, Drew’s dad is getting closer and closer to finding out his big secret. There is a lot going on. <br><br>Fable is such a kick ass heroine. She is strong, supportive, and carries the weight of the world on her shoulders. I was so happy Drew was able to step it up and be there for her this book. She needs someone she can count on. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ll always save you. You never have to worry about that.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Drew... I was so happy to see Drew overcome parts of his past and really start to heal. He made a ton of progress. Drew is just the total package. I mean, a sexy football star who writes poetry for his girl? I love it! <br><br>The story was great! We got introduced to some new characters (Jen and Colin... getting their own book I hear? I hope so!) Now back to Drew and Fable... they couldn't keep their hands off one another in this book! This book was definitely hotter than the last! Trust me- I’m not complaining! One of my favorite parts was the strip True Confessions game they played ;-) And it may be morbid to say... but I was really happy <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[With what happened with Adele! Glad she is finally out of the picture for good!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>And the ending... OMG this was the most perfect thing...<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <b>M</b>ost of the time I’m thinking of you<br><b>A</b>ll the time I love you<br><b>R</b>emembering the good times and the bad<br><b>S</b>o much has <br><b>H</b>appened and<br><b>M</b>aybe I’m moving too fast<br><b>A</b>ll I know is I...<br><b>L</b>ove you. And want to<br><b>L</b>ive with you <br><b>O</b>nly you<br><b>W</b>ill you be my wife? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>If you haven’t read One Week Girlfriend, pick it up, then read this one! It was amazing! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/SecondChanceBoyfriend-coupleredone_zps32db66c7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_566058598" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/566058598" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/566058598?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer566058598" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12726929255896619480"><b>4-4.5 STARS.</b><br/><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/443876.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><b>*I'm on a Drew Callahan Cloud Nine!!!*</b><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/403752.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><b>I loved him in the first book but now, he's also become a poet!?</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"For a passion that's<br/>Able to shine like ours<br/>Blessed are we to <br/>Love <br/>Each other."</i>
</b><br/><br/>And he had this^^ particular poem tattooed as a sign of his true love for Fable. How can you not love a guy who does a romantic gesture like that? Him alone, makes this book worth reading. Seriously. So, if you're going to read this series, prepare to *swoon* over him. Don't say I didn't warn y</span>
  <span id="freeText12726929255896619480" style="display:none"><b>4-4.5 STARS.</b><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/443876.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><b>*I'm on a Drew Callahan Cloud Nine!!!*</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/403752.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><b>I loved him in the first book but now, he's also become a poet!?</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"For a passion that's<br>Able to shine like ours<br>Blessed are we to <br>Love <br>Each other."</i>
</b><br><br>And he had this^^ particular poem tattooed as a sign of his true love for Fable. How can you not love a guy who does a romantic gesture like that? Him alone, makes this book worth reading. Seriously. So, if you're going to read this series, prepare to *swoon* over him. Don't say I didn't warn you! <br><br>Now, on to the review...<br><br><b>Second Chance Boyfriend</b> is the second part of the <b>Drew + Fable series</b> and I LOVED it even more than the first part!!! This series is the perfect relaxing, entertaining read with some very steamy scenes and a few unexpected turns that kept me glued to the pages the entire time I was reading it. Although I liked it even more than the first part of the series, I felt like "something" was missing for me to give it a five star rating, but still, I very much enjoyed reading this series and I would highly recommend anyone to give Drew and Fable's story a try!<br><br><br><b>Drew</b> - <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414113i/816096._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Drew I'm going to kick him in the balls next time I see him Callahan."</i>
</b><br><br>Yes, the way he left things at the end of the first part of the series, two months before the start of the second part, wasn't very smooth and it's perfectly understandable, Fable was furious with him for it. Although Drew seems like the guy who has it all together - he's extremely handsome, rich, has good grades and is the star football player in college - he's far from perfect. His past still haunts him and he's often still confronted with those issues in his present life. But Fable makes him want to change. She makes him want to address those problems and work on them in order to win her back.<br><br><b>"I've always run away in the past. But you, Fable. You make me want to stay."</b><br><br>Because for the first time in his life, Drew has found someone who makes him feel normal, who makes him feel anything at all. And he's not willing to let that go. I loved the fact that he was strong enough to face his old problems and that he was willing to embrace his love for Fable.<br><br><b>"She holds my heart in her hands. And for the first time in my life, I give it over to her completely. Freely. Fable Maguire owns me. And I know I own her too."</b><br><br><br><b>Fable</b> - <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414113i/816097.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Poor Fable... All she wanted was for for once, to be someone first choice. And with Drew, she thought she finally found what she'd been looking for...only to have it ripped from her hands all over again. So, after the way things ended between her and Drew, she tries to move on. She gets a new job, makes new friends but deep down, she's still hoping for her knight in shining armor to show back up in her life and sweep her off her feet.<br><br><b>"Drew Callahan is my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can't get enough of. He's my addiction and if I'm being honest with myself, I'm not looking to kick that particular habit anytime soon."</b><br><br>Her life isn't easy either. She has a lot of responsibilities to take care of, but she never complains about them. She's such a strong character with a personality that never backs down from anything and I loved the fact that she stood by Drew no matter what. Even when she discovered all of his darkest secrets, she never, not once, gave up on him.<br><br><b>Drew + Fable = PERFECT</b><br>They are both broken souls with a lot of baggage and a lot of drama in their live, but somehow they found each other amidst all of that and together they try to help each other through all the hard times. They still have a lot to learn about what it's like to be in a supportive relationship, but they're both willing to fall down and stand back up when things get rough. And that is what I loved about these two. Their relationship is real with real problems. It isn't always rainbows and butterflies but things aren't like that in real life either. But even when they were faced with difficult situations, they tried to make the best of it and they never gave up on believing in each other.<br><br><b>"Our relationship isn't perfect. Drew Callahan isn't perfect either. But I wouldn't have him any other way."</b><br><br><br>Other than that, I don't want to give away much more about the plot, because it might spoil too much. But, you should know, Adele makes an appearance again, one that doesn't go unnoticed. Oh, and there was one chapter in her point of view...<p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396859ra/765367.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p> Yeah, I didn't feel really comfortable reading that...BUT luckily it was a pretty short chapter!<br><br>I also loved some of the additional characters in this book, especially Fable's little brother Owen. I love how he always stood up for her, despite his young age. And I felt bad for the way their mom treated him. Then there were Colin, Fable's new boss, and Jenn, her new co-worker and friend. They seemed to have a thing going on between them (which I heard might be explored further in a new book?) and they definitely made the plot more interesting. But still, the main focus was on Drew and Fable and the undeniable attraction between these two and that is what I loved most about this book. Needless to say, it made me very happy to see these two get their <u>happily ever after</u>.<br><br><b>"Drew and I were never believers in the fairy tale. Now, we own the happily ever after and we refuse to let that bitch go." ~ Fable</b> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414113i/816098.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12726929255896619480" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13681051449366502581"><i>
  <b>I LOVED THIS BOOK MEGA LOTS!!!!</b>
</i><br/><br/>Holy hell this book was <i>
  <b>AWESOME!!!!</b>
</i> I'd give this one more stars if they were available. I love it when a book totally lives up to the hype and this sequel did that and more... It was everything I wanted it to be...<br/><br/>This one picks up about 2 months where <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17202452.One_Week_Girlfriend__Drew___Fable___1_' title='One Week Girlfriend (Drew + Fable, #1) by Monica Murphy' rel='nofollow noopener'>One Week Girlfriend</a> left off.. Drew and Fable are seperated and both very unhappy. Drew and Fable both come from very unstable families and we found out some extreamly heart wrenching things about Drew towar</span>
  <span id="freeText13681051449366502581" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>I LOVED THIS BOOK MEGA LOTS!!!!</b>
</i><br /><br />Holy hell this book was <i>
  <b>AWESOME!!!!</b>
</i> I'd give this one more stars if they were available. I love it when a book totally lives up to the hype and this sequel did that and more... It was everything I wanted it to be...<br /><br />This one picks up about 2 months where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17202452.One_Week_Girlfriend__Drew___Fable___1_" title="One Week Girlfriend (Drew + Fable, #1) by Monica Murphy" rel="nofollow noopener">One Week Girlfriend</a> left off.. Drew and Fable are seperated and both very unhappy. Drew and Fable both come from very unstable families and we found out some extreamly heart wrenching things about Drew towards the end of OWG. It leads Drew to think he's not good enough for Fable. He has one last beautiful night with her then leaves her with a note:<br /><br /><i><b>Dear Fable, <br />My worst enemy is behind me because of you.<br />And there’s still a lot left for me to explain. <br />Right now, all I can think about is you.<br />So many things in my life confuse me and…<br />Hurt me— except you. <br />Maybe we can be together again someday. <br />All I really want is you, but I can’t do this now.<br />Losing you will be the hardest thing I’ve dealt with yet.<br />Loving you might be a mistake. Drawing you intomy world will<br />Only hurt you. And I refuse to do that.<br />Will you ever forgive me?<i><br />~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ <br /><i>I love you.<br />Drew</i></i></b><br /><br /><br />MARSHMALLOW...the first letter in every sentence is their code word for each other that they need saving... Fable knew that Drew needed her and she tried for weeks to get him to see her but he ignored her. Now two months later and Fable is trying to move on but not doing a very good job of it. Neither is Drew. When they finally run in to each other the love is so clearly still there. The love these two felt for each other was just... beautiful. They were both everything that each other needed. They both needed saving. <br /><br />This book is the next part of their journey; them coming to understand the depth of their love for each other and be there for one another when the rest of their worlds are crumbling around them. I love how we did not have to wait long at all for them to get back together where they belong and the majority of this story is them dealing with all of thier outside issues together..TOGETHER. <br /><br />I simply could not stand to put this book down.. every page had me wrapped up in Drew and Fable. My heart just clenched and ached for both of them so much and then those special moments would happen when I just felt so much happy sappy good love and my heart would breath easy again. I love books hat do that--take hold of you and don't let go until the very end. I had a huge smile on my face at the end. Such an awesome awesome story. <br /><br />If you've not read Drew and Fable's story you need to get busy.. they are totally worth your time.. And to Moncia Murphey-- PLEASE get us a story for Jen and Colin!! <br /><br /><br /><br /></i></span>

    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/526548432?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer526548432" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16408621233395869953"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408161i/798262._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Drew Callahan is my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can’t get enough of. He’s my addiction and if I’m being honest with myself, I’m not looking to kick that particular habit anytime soon.”~ Fable </i>
</b><br/><br/>Second Chance Boyfriend is a fast paced, sexy, romantic, wonderful sequel! <br/><br/>This book picks up with both Drew and Fable feeling the loss after Drew leaves her “the note” at the end of the first book. This story is told in alternating POVS of Drew and Fable with a shocking POV from the evil stepmoth</span>
  <span id="freeText16408621233395869953" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408161i/798262._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”Drew Callahan is my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can’t get enough of. He’s my addiction and if I’m being honest with myself, I’m not looking to kick that particular habit anytime soon.”~ Fable </i>
</b><br><br>Second Chance Boyfriend is a fast paced, sexy, romantic, wonderful sequel! <br><br>This book picks up with both Drew and Fable feeling the loss after Drew leaves her “the note” at the end of the first book. This story is told in alternating POVS of Drew and Fable with a shocking POV from the evil stepmother. <br><br>Drew is sexy and sweet and Fable is kick ass and fantastic. As a couple, they have it all!<br><br>I was expecting Monica Murphy to torture me with the wait for Drew and Fable to get back together but...NOPE. Fable is offered a new job from a hot restaurant owner which left me nervous for about two seconds until Drew comes in with his fellow teammates and sees Fable. Drew is working with a therapist and has come a long way in his ability to face his problems head on. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I’ve always run away in the past. But you, Fable. You make me want to stay."~Drew</i>
</b><br><br>Between Drew’s father and evil stepmother and Fable’s mother our couple gets through some heavy situations but they do it together. <br> <br>There were many sexy scenes that weren’t drawn out or over the top… they were just plain <b>HOT</b>! Dirty-Talking, True Confessions Game, and the club scene I just loved!! On a sweet note, Drew’s poems were completely swoon worthy!! <br><br>My guess is Jennifer and Colin may possibly get a book? <br><br>I loved the epilogue and I couldn’t be happier with the ending. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408161i/798263._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Now, we own the happily ever after and we refuse to let that bitch go." ~Fable</i>
</b><br><br>Bravo Monica Murphy!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16408621233395869953" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13272060600622163844">Where do I start with this amazing story other than SQUEE!!!<br/><br/>Okay, so this is not a review based on expectation. I have READ Second Chance Boyfriend. I read it even before it went to the editor. As a long-time friend and critique partner of the amaaaaazing Monica Murphy, I have the ultimate BEST FRIEND JOB IN THE WORLD of reading her delicious books before everyone else does! That's right! I get to see them get born and watch their magical journey, every. Single. Time!<br/><br/>And I have to tell all of yo</span>
  <span id="freeText13272060600622163844" style="display:none">Where do I start with this amazing story other than SQUEE!!!<br /><br />Okay, so this is not a review based on expectation. I have READ Second Chance Boyfriend. I read it even before it went to the editor. As a long-time friend and critique partner of the amaaaaazing Monica Murphy, I have the ultimate BEST FRIEND JOB IN THE WORLD of reading her delicious books before everyone else does! That's right! I get to see them get born and watch their magical journey, every. Single. Time!<br /><br />And I have to tell all of you waiting for SECOND CHANCE BOYFRIEND - this book will rock your socks off as much or even more than ONE WEEK GIRLFRIEND. It is amazing! I'd give it more stars, if I could!<br /><br />Right from the start, there's the longing, the angst, the palpable love between them - and yet, the obstacles. Among them, that damn woman Adele. *shudder*<br /><br />I couldn't wait for them to overcome the obstacles, let down their walls, and just be with each other! So I truly can't begin to express how heart-wrenching and beautiful it was to watch Drew and Fable reconnect. I drank up every word they said to each other and melted with each one. Then . . . it is HOT. Hotter even than OWG. Oh my god! And the drama! Adele! I hate that woman so! I won't spoil this incredible read, but Monica blew my mind. Nothing could have prepared me for the climax. This book is a fantastic, emotional, angsty, sexy, dramatic, whoppingly romantic read that will leave you breathless and wanting to scream MARSHMAHLLOW!!! <br /><br />SECOND CHANCE BOYFRIEND, I just can't wait for the world to read it and love it like I do!</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_588869682" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/588869682" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588869682?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588869682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5703644574560346289"><b>WOW WOW WOW!!!!! Loved it!!!!!</b><br/><b>FIREWORKS AND A MARCHING BAND SHOULD FOLLOW THE ENDING TO THIS BOOK!</b><br/><br/>Before you start this review, if you haven’t read One-Week Girlfriend, stop right now and go read it. You will not be disappointed!!!! This book is a continuation of the story, so there may be some spoilers included from the first book. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>Two people in love, alone, isolated from the world, that’s beautiful. –Milan Kundera</i>
</b><br/><br/>So this book begins at the end of One Week Girlfriend, well actually 2 months</span>
  <span id="freeText5703644574560346289" style="display:none"><b>WOW WOW WOW!!!!! Loved it!!!!!</b><br><b>FIREWORKS AND A MARCHING BAND SHOULD FOLLOW THE ENDING TO THIS BOOK!</b><br><br>Before you start this review, if you haven’t read One-Week Girlfriend, stop right now and go read it. You will not be disappointed!!!! This book is a continuation of the story, so there may be some spoilers included from the first book. <br><br><b>
  <i>Two people in love, alone, isolated from the world, that’s beautiful. –Milan Kundera</i>
</b><br><br>So this book begins at the end of One Week Girlfriend, well actually 2 months later, following the heartbreaking note that Drew left for Fable after their last night together. She has tried contacting him several times since, but has gotten no response. She is still wants to believe he cares for her after that incredibly heart felt note he left her with, but still…who does that?<br><br><b>
  <i>Who spends the most intense week of their life with another human being and shares their most intimate thoughts, their craziest, darkest secrets, has sex with a person – and we’re talking amazing, earth-shattering sex –leaves them a note that says I love you and then bails?</i>
</b><br><br>Well apparently Drew Fucking Callahan, that’s who!!! Fable is left feeling very conflicted, and once again losing the fragile trust she was finally building with him. So what does she do? She does what Fable Maguire always does; she picks up the pieces and moves on. Back to her life, back to her responsibilities. But this time, she can’t seem to shake him. She can’t stop thinking of him, wondering what he is doing, and how he is coping with all of the shit going on in his life. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Sometimes you have to stand alone, just to make sure you still can.” –Unknown</i>
</b><br><br>But true to her ways, she accepts her fate, she puts him out of her thoughts and she moves on with her life. Until one night, working at LaSalle’s, she meets Colin. A devastatingly handsome guy who sweeps her off her feet and into a new job at the hottest new restaurant in town…The District. But while Fable finds him very attractive, she still can’t quite get a read on him, and she is very hesitant to accept his kindness. She is constantly feeling scrutinized by him. His suggestions for personal improvement, and his generosity to pay for them are both admirable and insulting to her. But Fable goes along with it all, in the name of a better job, more money, and the hope for a better future.<br><br><b>
  <i>”So why did you hire me?” “I saw your potential,” he said softly. “Do you, Fable? Do you see it?” I couldn’t answer him. Because the truth wasn’t what he wanted to hear. No. </i>
</b><br><br>Then there’s Drew. He has tried to move on too, but the poor guy is still heartbroken. He is still dreaming of the girl that changed his life, the girl that changed him… in only one short week together. But he is still convinced that she is better off without him, that she is too good for him. <br><br>I just loved reading Drew’s POV. He is just SUCH A GOOD GUY!!!! A romantic. Those poems he kept playing with…. So damn SWOONY!!!! Drew may have been a bit messed up in his head, but let me tell you… there was absolutely NOTHING wrong with this boys heart!!!!! And his tattoo…sooooo sweet!!!!!! Fable hit the freaking lotto with this guy. <br><br><b>
  <i>M</i>
</b>aybe it was a mistake leaving you.<br><b>A</b>nd I don’t know how to make it right.<br><b>R</b>egret fills me every single day.<br><b>S</b>o much of it builds up I<br><b>H</b>ate myself for<br><b>M</b>issing you. Hurting you.<br><b>A</b>nd I want you to know I…<br><b>L</b>ong for you<br><b>L</b>ove you<br><b>O</b>thers may come and go in our lives but…<br><b>W</b>e belong together<br><br>SWOOOOOOOOOOOOOONNNNNNNNNN!!!!!!!!!!!!! Seriously, I’m totally in love with Drew!!!!! I think the only thing he did wrong was to beat himself up over things that weren’t even his fault. He was always quick to blame himself for every problem. But still, it didn’t make him weak… he was still possessive and jealous, and even a bit forceful at times… which was a TOTAL turn-on!!!!! OK, have I gushed enough…I think so.<br><br><b>
  <i>She holds my heart in her hands. And for the first time in my life, I give it over to her completely. Freely. Fable Maguire owns me. And I know I own her.</i>
</b><br><br>Now I have to say, Fable did irritate me occasionally throughout the book. She was a little moody and irrationally bitchy at times… but I got over it….but only because she got over it. ;)<br><br>Now, without expounding on anything from the story, I will say that the story dragged just a little in the middle. Not to say there wasn't some smoking hot sex between these two. They have such an amazing chemistry together. And there is still some innocence to the couple that is just beautiful!!!! <br><br>But, I was waiting for something explosive to happen, and it just didn’t….until….IT DID!!!!!! But it wasn’t until the end that I was just fucking BLOWN AWAY!!!<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[no pun intended!!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>I have to say, the last 20% of this book was just fantastic!!!!!! I was shocked, pissed, and fucking jumping for joy all in about 30 minutes time. My updates speak for themselves. I think I woke my husband 3 or 4 times cursing out-loud or typing furiously…my horrific updates!!!!! I even made a new GR friend at 1am who couldn’t help but respond to my constant cyber shouts of pain and ire!!!! <br><br>And in the end….the author GOT IT RIGHT!!!!!!!!!!! She ended this the ONLY WAY it could have worked for me!!!!!!!! AND I FUCKING LOVED THE ENDING TO THIS BOOK!!!!!!!!! It actually changed my rating from 4 to 5 stars!!! And completely deserved it!!! <br><br>I highly recommend this series… but if you are going to read the first book… you HAVE to read the second one…MANDATORY!!!!<br><br>Major spoiler...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[

    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11588440-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451259033p2/11588440.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525737410?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/11588440-amy">Amy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525737410" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4964213850537983493">You know how there are just some authors whose writing style just “clicks” for you. It’s so effortless and easy to read. You find yourself sitting down to read ONE chapter and the next thing you know, it’s 3 hours later and you’ve completely ignored all those things you were supposed to do today. Yeah, Monica Murphy is one of those people for me. I devoured both One Week Girlfriend and Second Chance Boyfriend and loved them both.<br/><br/>This book picks up right where One Week Girlfriend ended. Drew and </span>
  <span id="freeText4964213850537983493" style="display:none">You know how there are just some authors whose writing style just “clicks” for you. It’s so effortless and easy to read. You find yourself sitting down to read ONE chapter and the next thing you know, it’s 3 hours later and you’ve completely ignored all those things you were supposed to do today. Yeah, Monica Murphy is one of those people for me. I devoured both One Week Girlfriend and Second Chance Boyfriend and loved them both.<br /><br />This book picks up right where One Week Girlfriend ended. Drew and Fable are no longer together, though neither one has really moved on. They are both so broken and still dealing with their terrible family situations. My heart broke for Drew and all he went through with Adele. I was so proud of him for taking it upon himself to find a therapist and get the help he needs. And the tattoo he got for Fable, I was majorly swooning. He’s got such a good heart and I just loved him. Excellent conclusion to Drew and Fable’s story!!	<br /><br />And thanks to Tessa at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bookswinefood.blogspot.com">http://bookswinefood.blogspot.com</a> for gifting me a copy of this book :)</span>

<div id="review_578682934" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578682934" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/578682934?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=college">college</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578682934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8364719945826164455"><b>
  <i>1.5 STARS </i>
</b><br/><br/>2 consecutive chucks to the dnf pile is a no-no for me so I stuck with this one until the painful end. Which means churning out this review was excruciating.<br/><br/>I read <i>One Week Girlfriend</i> as part of a group challenge and remember liking it enough because of Drew's screwed up, soapy past. I really wanted to know how his secret will hit the fan. I also remember my Monica Murphy Reading Experience to be quite pleasant with very little cringe-worthy moments.<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/SAihcHA' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415943ra/821352.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>For a passion that's<br/>Able to </i></span>
  <span id="freeText8364719945826164455" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>1.5 STARS </i>
</b><br><br>2 consecutive chucks to the dnf pile is a no-no for me so I stuck with this one until the painful end. Which means churning out this review was excruciating.<br><br>I read <i>One Week Girlfriend</i> as part of a group challenge and remember liking it enough because of Drew's screwed up, soapy past. I really wanted to know how his secret will hit the fan. I also remember my Monica Murphy Reading Experience to be quite pleasant with very little cringe-worthy moments.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/SAihcHA" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415943ra/821352.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>For a passion that's<br>Able to shine like ours<br>Blessed are we to<br>Love<br>Each other </i><br><br>That's breakfast right there: Hammy AND cheesy.<br><br>I don't know, maybe my heart really is a giant block of ice or maybe I'm missing a few bits and bobs on the part of the brain that should make me melt over these romantic literary feats but my gag reflex is just a wee bit too ticklish, I feel. These juvenile efforts to make me get hot and bothered over Drew just ended up with me bothered.<br><br>The book picks up 2 months after the end of OWG. I'm not sure where Murphy was going to take Drew and Fable's story but I wasn't expecting to bitch and moan over the seam-ful writing. Arguments got rambling and repetitive and the use of the "we'll talk later" plot device was used to the extreme. Can't you just resolve an issue once it arises so you can make up new ones instead of drawing out the argument for a hundred or so pages? It's bad enough that the paper-thin plot was stretched to absurd limits but to be perpetually stuck in the same discussion written with such an immature POV was just exhausting.<br><br><i>
  <b>I look at Drew. No way am I going to say anything to Owen about... that. "She's a little mentally unstable at the moment. Everyone's worried about her." Ick. I can't believe I just said that. I'm not worried about her. <u>I wish she'd fall off the face of the earth and rot in hell forever.</u></b>
</i><br><br>Are we sure Fable's not in fifth grade?<br><br>The new secondary characters (save for Drew's therapist, who sounded like the only sensible person in the story) felt rudimentary: what was the point of Colin and Jen? Colin was supposed to be the enigmatic boss who has faith in Fable's capabilities but by the end of the book <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Fable was still a waitress in his restaurant, so why is he in this story again and why didn't Fable just stick with her old job? I would've gladly taken him as the token other-guy in a love triangle <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> just so he'd have some use.<br><br>The only thing I was looking forward to was resolved too conveniently. While others might have gotten squicked by it, I found <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Drew's affair with his stepmom and possibly fathering his supposed younger sister <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> made the first book original and intriguing (though certainly some messed up, sh*t). How it was tackled in this book felt like it threw away the one interesting thing it had going for it. The way Adele acted was completely ridiculous and out of her conniving, devious character (mostly because there was really no effort to develop her beyond the evil stepmom here). <br><br>Drew's efforts to be a man worthy of Fable (outside the poems, anyway) and Fable's relationship with Owen and her mother would've been more interesting to me than the pedestrian sex scenes which automatically follows the "we'll talk later"s. I'm not even going to speculate how they'd fare as a couple beyond the last chapter since everything gets resolved with sex anyway so they OBVIOUSLY have a great happily ever after ahead of them.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8364719945826164455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525293647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1259642606578124318"><b>5</b>--Thank-you for not making us wait forever for Drew + Fable to get back together--<b>Stars</b>!<br/><br/><b>5</b>--Drew is so sexy, sweet, funny, generous and caring--<b>Stars</b>!!!<br/><br/>Did I mention how much I <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407721ra/796680.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> Drew!!! No really! I am IN LOVE with Drew! <br/><br/>Second Chance Boyfriend was the perfect conclusion to Drew + Fable's love story! I loved every minute of it....the good and the bad. As I mentioned before, I am so glad Ms. Murphy didn't make us wait ages for Drew + Fable to get back together. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/452214.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story begins with Fable working</span>
  <span id="freeText1259642606578124318" style="display:none"><b>5</b>--Thank-you for not making us wait forever for Drew + Fable to get back together--<b>Stars</b>!<br><br><b>5</b>--Drew is so sexy, sweet, funny, generous and caring--<b>Stars</b>!!!<br><br>Did I mention how much I <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407721ra/796680.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Drew!!! No really! I am IN LOVE with Drew! <br><br>Second Chance Boyfriend was the perfect conclusion to Drew + Fable's love story! I loved every minute of it....the good and the bad. As I mentioned before, I am so glad Ms. Murphy didn't make us wait ages for Drew + Fable to get back together. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/452214.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story begins with Fable working at a new restaurant and has a new hottie boss (I was a little worried about where this storyline might go). Drew is seeing a therapist and trying to work on his issues. He shows at the restaurant for a party and it was all over from there. <br><br>One look, one touch, one kiss and Drew + Fable realize that they can't live without each other. The chemistry between Drew + Fable was electric....sparks flying off of the page. It was HOT. Drew promises he's not going to run anymore. He's going to be open and honest and allow Fable to be there for him. <br><br>Unfortunately, Adele (that evil skank bitch) hasn't gone away and Fable's mom continues to be her worthless self. But Drew + Fable work through their problems together....strengthening their relationship along the way. <br><br>Drew! Yes, he needs his own paragraph. Drew was so sweet and sensitive. Caring and loving. Sexy and romantic. He was perfection, flaws and all. His poems...gah! <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>DREW......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/429028.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the ending and that Drew was able to get closure. The only closure I didn't seem to get was for Fable--with her mom and Owen. But word on the street is Owen will be getting his own book...so I am excited to see where Drew + Fable are and what happens to Owen. <br><br>And to conclude.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407970ra/797495.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<div id="review_544737327" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/544737327" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454474452p2/9816167.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/544737327?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review">Jessica&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544737327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer320943778010593528"><a href='http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Read more reviews at Jessica’s Book Review</a><br/><a href='https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find Me on Facebook</a><br/><br/><b>"For a passion that's<br/>Able to shine like ours<br/>Blessed are we to <br/>Love <br/>Each other." </b><br/><br/>I adored One Week Girlfriend, like a lot… like a lot, a lot, a lot. I loved the character of Fable and her strong will. Drew is another great character who seems to have it all, a big football star, wealthy, and very good looking but holding onto a big dark secret that no one knows, until Fable comes into his world. They were amazing together and the ending</span>
  <span id="freeText320943778010593528" style="display:none"><a href="http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Read more reviews at Jessica’s Book Review</a><br /><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview" rel="nofollow noopener">Find Me on Facebook</a><br /><br /><b>"For a passion that's<br />Able to shine like ours<br />Blessed are we to <br />Love <br />Each other." </b><br /><br />I adored One Week Girlfriend, like a lot… like a lot, a lot, a lot. I loved the character of Fable and her strong will. Drew is another great character who seems to have it all, a big football star, wealthy, and very good looking but holding onto a big dark secret that no one knows, until Fable comes into his world. They were amazing together and the ending of OWG left you in shock and so mad at Drew. I couldn’t wait to get my hands on Second Chance Boyfriend and hopefully Drew figures his crazy step-mom issues out and step up to be the mad Fable deserves and who he really is. So of course when SCG was released I read it and had it read within in hours.<br /><br />Second Chance Boyfriend picks up a few months after where OWG left off. Drew had left Fable after sharing a very passionate and confessing one week with her. Once they return to their town Drew leaves Fable in a note stating he cannot be with her. SCB is again in both Fable &amp; Drew’s POV; I love that I am able to get into both their heads and know how they feel about each other. <br /><br />The roles were a bit revered in SCB. I felt Drew helped Fable a lot more in this book when previously Fable helped Drew cope with his Step Mother, Adele. He really stepped up in this book compared to the last book; he wanted Fable, wouldn’t let her go, and even fought for her. I enjoyed him so much more in SCB, he grew up and changed a lot since he walked away from Fable. I felt like I was given closure to all the craziness of Adele and Drew from the last book. I agree with the author that I felt sad for Adele by the end; I know I shouldn’t but I did. Though she is not in the book much she gave me the total creeps still! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>He needs me now more than ever. I hope I can be enough for him. I hope we can be enough for each other.</i>
</b><br /><br />I don’t think I felt the spark in this book that I did in One Week Weekend. I guess I prefer the crazy drama a bit more. Yes there was drama in SCB, don’t get me wrong just not really until the end and even that did not last very long, I was hoping it was a bit more of the story. I do love the relationship Drew &amp; Fable now have. It seems healthy and stable, something they both need desperately. I really hope their story continues. I would love to see them get married, have babies and live happily ever after. <br /><br />Drew was never on my book boyfriend radar but he sure is now! Drew and his poetry can do whatever they want to me! I’m on the Drew fan train now!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’ll always save you. You never have to worry about that.”</i>
</b><br /><br />I give Second Chance Boyfriend 3 Stars<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="320943778010593528" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_663951219" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/663951219" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/663951219?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer663951219" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12555622913910179574"><b>****Spoilers ahead for those who haven’t read One Week Girlfriend****</b><br/><br/>Second Chance Boyfriend was a perfect ending to the Drew+Fable story! I adored these characters and their emotional story in One Week Girlfriend, so I picked this up as soon as I finished OWG. <br/><br/>Our story picks up two months after One Week Girlfriend with Fable heartbroken and trying to move on after Drew basically dropped off the planet two months ago. You can’t really blame Drew, because seriously this guy had a whopper of a re</span>
  <span id="freeText12555622913910179574" style="display:none"><b>****Spoilers ahead for those who haven’t read One Week Girlfriend****</b><br /><br />Second Chance Boyfriend was a perfect ending to the Drew+Fable story! I adored these characters and their emotional story in One Week Girlfriend, so I picked this up as soon as I finished OWG. <br /><br />Our story picks up two months after One Week Girlfriend with Fable heartbroken and trying to move on after Drew basically dropped off the planet two months ago. You can’t really blame Drew, because seriously this guy had a whopper of a revelation from that evil witch Adele!! <b>HATE HER!!!</b> Rest assured the pain doesn’t last for long and we are soothed and consumed with <i>lusty</i> moments and <i>steamy</i> scenes! Oh Drew and Fable are such a magnetic couple and their desire for each other is <i>palpable</i> and so very sweet!! I reveled in their happiness, because these two deserve it!! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>God, he is so stinking cute and he’s all mine. Mine, mine, mine. We’re pretending we’re perfectly normal and we’re not. We’re both all sorts of messed up….<br />More than anything, I know I love him. And Drew loves me. Even though we haven’t said it to each other yet, I know deep in my heart it’s the truth. </i>
</b><br /><br />This is not to say there weren’t bumps in the road, how can there not be with the situations Drew and Fable have to deal with. I will say that I was entirely happy with what happened to Adele in the end. Does that make me evil and unfeeling? Maybe, but I don’t care! She was not sorry and let’s face it, she would do it again given another opportunity! *shudders* She’s a train wreck waiting to destroy another’s life. So, no, I’m not sorry for how I felt about what happened to her!! <br /><br />My heart soared reading Drew and Fable’s lovely and moving romance!! *sigh* It was an utterly satisfying conclusion! Monica Murphy has been put on my “automatic buy list” after finishing! She managed to sweep me up with her intense and compelling story! <br /><br />I just met the author at an event, and I’m happy to report that we’ll get a novella of them in the future! And we have a companion novel centering on Jen and Colin’s story, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17969384.Three_Broken_Promises__Drew___Fable___3_" title="Three Broken Promises (Drew + Fable, #3) by Monica Murphy" rel="nofollow noopener">Three Broken Promises</a>, set to release December 10th of this year. I can’t wait!!</span>

The ending was hurtful and broken, Drew leaves Fable because he believes he is unworthy of love. 2 months have passed and Drew has not contacted Fable. She is struggling to move on with her life. He broke her heart and moving on is not as easy as it seems, really not as easy for Drew either.<br/><br/>Meet Drew- <b>I'm going to kick him in the balls next time I see</b></span>

Fable gets a new job with a fabulous boss, just when she things that maybe she can start moving on, Drew comes to the new restaurant where she is working.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/38ae1e59-4989-4efb-966d-2b8699f869e9_zpsaf3b70de.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>They do come together to rekindle their love. This is their story of love that they thought was lost but deep down they both knew they were the one for one another. They are both from troubled past, one so much more than the other, but can they be there for one another? Can they trust that no one will run again? This story is sweet, beautiful, loving, hurtful, remorseful, hopeful, tragic and a fantastic love story. Drew and Fable are a young and all inspiring couple. Are they able to overcome so much hurt from their past? They have to work and trust, but it's a beautiful story that leaves your heart in the most happiest of places.         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=emotional-roller-coaster">emotional-roller-coaster</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer738587010" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer445613307314911928"><strong>****4 Awwww Stars****</strong><br/><br/>This book ends the saga of Drew and Fable.  It has been a wonderful and full of drama ride but the ending surely made it worth it.<br/><br/>The author has a way of one minute making you want to cry and in the next second you are swooning. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381535022i/4995185.jpg' alt='' width='407' height='354' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After "One Week Girlfriend" we left Fable broken hearted because Drew left her.  This story opens up with a  very confused Drew who sucks at football and is emotionally tortured.  Fable and Drew go through more and more obstacles in their relationshi</span>
  <span id="freeText445613307314911928" style="display:none"><strong>****4 Awwww Stars****</strong><br><br>This book ends the saga of Drew and Fable.  It has been a wonderful and full of drama ride but the ending surely made it worth it.<br><br>The author has a way of one minute making you want to cry and in the next second you are swooning. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381535022i/4995185.jpg" alt="" width="407" height="354" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After "One Week Girlfriend" we left Fable broken hearted because Drew left her.  This story opens up with a  very confused Drew who sucks at football and is emotionally tortured.  Fable and Drew go through more and more obstacles in their relationship and their love is tested around every corner.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381535022ra/4995186.gif" alt="" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I fell in love with Drew and loved how Fable was the foundation in their relationship.  This was definitely a heartfelt book that had me wishing for more at the end.</span>
