<div id="review_552115549" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/552115549" />
    <a title="Autumn Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review"><img alt="Autumn Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399327915p2/6908049.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/552115549?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Autumn Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Autumn Review" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review">Autumn Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552115549" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18111071321713591946">Drew Callahan is my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can't get enough of. He's my addiction and if I'm being honest with myself, I'm not looking to kick that particular habit anytime soon.<br/><br/>Umm...yep. That pretty much sums up my review. I have to say that it's been a while since I fell completely head over heels in love with a character. Drew Callahan. I just love him. Not only do I love Drew, but I really love Fable. Drew and Fable together give a great example of what unconditional love should b</span>
  <span id="freeText18111071321713591946" style="display:none">Drew Callahan is my absolute weakness. Like a drug I can't get enough of. He's my addiction and if I'm being honest with myself, I'm not looking to kick that particular habit anytime soon.<br /><br />Umm...yep. That pretty much sums up my review. I have to say that it's been a while since I fell completely head over heels in love with a character. Drew Callahan. I just love him. Not only do I love Drew, but I really love Fable. Drew and Fable together give a great example of what unconditional love should be like. <br /><br />At the end of One Week Girlfriend, I was in tears. Drew and Fable had reached a level in their relationship that I thought nothing could shake. However, Drew really had a lot of healing to do. Second Chance Boyfriend really showed both characters in a vulnerable light. Drew finally realizes he needs to make some changes in his life or else he will never be able to escape his past. And really, Fable was going through the same thing. What makes this book so great is that, despite the hardships they face individually, they were really there for each other as a couple. <br /><br />Another thing that made this book so great were the secondary characters. We get to know Fable's brother, Owen a bit better and I'll say this right now...I want a book for him. He needs a book. That kid has a story to tell. Also, near the end of the book, I was surprised to say that Colin, who is Fable's boss, grew on me. I felt like I got to know him better and his past intrigues me. Of course, I can't mention Colin without mentioning Jen. Together, I think those two will make a great couple and that their book will be pretty hot!<br /><br />Overall, I'm absolutely grateful that I found Drew + Fable's books. They are without a doubt, two of my favorite books of this year! Their story and their love for each other just pulls you in. You root for them, cry for them, laugh with them, and fall in love with them. I delayed reading the last chapter because I wasn't ready for their story to end. The only thing that made it better was knowing that we will possibly get to see glimpses of Drew + Fable in companion novels. *Crosses fingers* If you haven't read this beautiful and gripping series, you must go NOW and read them! <br /><br />Quotes:<br />~He asks me to rescue him and then he ditches me. Tells me he loves me in a note and never replies to my calls or texts. He's a jerk. <br />He's an asshole.<br />I'm in love with a jerky asshole and damn, that's painful to admit.-Loc 619<br /><br />~"Fine. I've always run away in the past. But you, Fable. You make me want to stay."-Loc 1517<br /><br />~She holds my heart in her hands. And for the first time in my life, I give it over to her completely.<br />Freely.<br />Fable Maguire owns me. And I know I own her.-Loc 3246<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18111071321713591946" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_525195704" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525195704" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525195704?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17791803-second-chance-boyfriend">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=continuing-plot">continuing-plot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=april-2013">april-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525195704" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3901375494235305744">Fantastic conclusion to a very beautiful story.<br/><br/>I loved this book. I liked it even more than the first, and I really liked the first.<br/><br/>The book starts of around 2 months after the first one ended.<br/><br/>Drew and Fable are both dealing with the fallout of the events that took place at the end of One Week Girlfriend.<br/><br/>I really liked that Drew had made his own decision to seek professional help and see a therapist. He had a long road to recovery, but it was realistic and heart-breaking to read. <br/><br/>I was a bit thr</span>
  <span id="freeText3901375494235305744" style="display:none">Fantastic conclusion to a very beautiful story.<br><br>I loved this book. I liked it even more than the first, and I really liked the first.<br><br>The book starts of around 2 months after the first one ended.<br><br>Drew and Fable are both dealing with the fallout of the events that took place at the end of One Week Girlfriend.<br><br>I really liked that Drew had made his own decision to seek professional help and see a therapist. He had a long road to recovery, but it was realistic and heart-breaking to read. <br><br>I was a bit thrown off by the introduction of Colin, Fable's new boss. He came off as a total creeper at first with comments on Fable changing her looks. I was very confused by his character for the entire book. He makes a comment to Drew when he first meets him that made me think that Colin was interested in Fable in a way that went beyong employee and boss. But at the end they are all friends all of a sudden. It was a very strange development for me. Towards the end we see that there might be something between Colin and Jen, Fable's coworker. But I felt that it totally came out of left field. <br><br>The rest of the book was fantastic. It was steamy and beautiful. I loved Drew's tattoo and the development of their relationship.<br><br>The events that take place at the end though<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407955ra/797430.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy shocker batman! Even though some of them I saw coming...one threw me for a loop completely and shocked the bejebus out of me!<br><br>I adored the epilogue. I found myself tearing up while reading it. I swear, it could have been so cheesy, but instead it was so cute! I just loved it.<br><br>5+ stars <br><br>I am now a huge fan of Monica Murphy and cannot wait for her future books<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3901375494235305744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6J6QQZY8tRU2mp8PSjIwEHF9yF0Fc9stMv7kQk9y9VShS2edORnFssUZ5GFISZT80LKg3HQ70a3ZFIjpLu8KpA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CCfk798l7DRyrROowA+vyr5he/CQJnCmYKYTZe+1PUVB8hMzcACck4EuaMbCdAsmH64TceFueiaLTH/OjijCtQ==')})
  }
